<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:under.html>under</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">untar</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:under.html>under</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saxon.html>Saxon</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">undar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hunsrik" class="extiw" title="w:Hunsrik">Hunsrik</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hrx">unne</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:under.html>under</a></i>).
